name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Standard Room With City View
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Family
info:1 Review
rating:5
posted:Posted May 7, 2024
msg:I have stayed in many five-star hotels at home and abroad, but this is the first time that a hotel will call to consult guests about their needs as soon as they book a room!
During the entire stay, I can feel that the hotel staff is well trained and has a strong sense of service. Because I have been traveling around Japan and other cities in China in the past month, the hotel has two very pleasant experiences in accommodation.
There are two points in the hotel that are particularly worth staying in, one is the food and beverage, and the other is that the bedding is very comfortable, soft and smooth, and I really want to buy it back.

The experience of just arriving in Nanning was not pleasant. I parked in the hotel parking lot, and before I got off the car, I was scratched by a local car that came to the hotel for dinner. The other party did not cooperate with the damage assessment and spoke wildly. I wanted to call the traffic police for almost an hour. But the experience of staying in was still very good. When we learned that we had an accident inside the hotel and the insurance had not been completed, the front desk took the initiative to help us check whether the vehicle was also staying in the hotel, and gave us the hotel's own snacks as souvenirs to comfort us.

During the May Day holiday, Nanning hotels were very tight. We booked a 2.7-meter king-size bed room and two 1.35-meter twin beds for three days.

Environment: The hotel is located next to the Shaomai Exhibition Center in Nanning. Exit A of the Exhibition Center is Haoyang City, which is very convenient for shopping and eating. Crossing the road is Hangyang City, which is very convenient for shopping and eating. It is also very close to Nanning East Station by a subway station from Mixc.

Hygiene: The hotel's hygiene is quite good. The daily cleaning is done very well. The clothes we hung in the closet also helped us turn them to the top of the bathtub, so that the clothes can dry faster.

Facilities: There are sufficient underground parking lots and ground parking spaces, and the management is good. There is a 24-hour restaurant inside the hotel. We went to the restaurant to eat on the first day when it rained, and we didn't need to go out in the rain. The price is affordable and the food is delicious. The hotel has a large swimming pool, and the children have a lot of fun. The hotel itself is not particularly new, and the furniture is good, but it is relatively old-fashioned. The room has a bathtub, which is very comfortable and convenient for bathing a baby.

Service: The service is very good. When we checked in, we saw that we had a lot of luggage and helped us transport it. If we needed to add spare parts, we would respond quickly and deliver them. The check-in and check-out were very fast, and they were very considerate to our needs.

Catering: The hotel's catering is really delicious, including homemade snacks.
There are many types of breakfast, including many Guangxi-style snacks, such as snail noodles, Laoyou noodles, oil tea, and soy milk. There is also a triangular roll of noodles with water chestnuts in it? Pour gravy on it, it is very delicious.
The restaurant next to the hotel is also very delicious. Seeing this kind of 24-hour restaurant, I feel that the people of Nanning are so happy. I haven't seen morning tea on a cart for a long time. It's so happy to have a night tea in the middle of the night.
I ate the souvenirs given to me after leaving the hotel. The egg yolk crisps in it are really delicious. If it's in the store, I will buy two more boxes.
